      <div class="aem-margin-options" id="if76202d588cf58fde24360b57aba0210">
       <style>
        /* CSS */
.author-instructions {
    font-weight: bold;
    text-transform: uppercase;
    color: red;
}

.wcm-publish .author-instructions {
    display: none;
}


/* To fix the buy now button being way too big at mobile */
@media(max-width: 719px) {
    .price-atc .content-ctn .price-atc-cta.size-normal a {
        padding: 12px 24px;
        font-size: 12px;
    }
}

/* To fix checkerboard copy alignment problems */
.checkerboard-row .copy {
    padding-left: 0;
    padding-right: 0;
}

/* To fix tech specs having way too much bottom padding in Safari */
ul.tech-specs {
    display: block;
}

/* Checkerboard: to make it so symmetric has a bg colour */
/* LOGIWEB-1558 */
@media(max-width: 719px) {
    .checkerboard[data-layout="symmetric"][data-theme-mobile="theme-light"] .media-portion,
    .checkerboard[data-layout="symmetric"][data-theme-mobile="theme-light"] .text-portion {
        background-color: #fff;
    }    
}
@media(min-width: 720px) and (max-width: 1024px) {
    .checkerboard[data-layout="symmetric"][data-theme-tablet="theme-light"] .media-portion,
    .checkerboard[data-layout="symmetric"][data-theme-tablet="theme-light"] .text-portion {
        background-color: #fff;
    } 
}
@media (min-width: 1025px) {
    .checkerboard[data-layout="symmetric"][data-theme-desktop="theme-light"] .checkerboard-row:not([data-layout="full"]) .media-portion,
    .checkerboard[data-layout="symmetric"][data-theme-desktop="theme-light"] .checkerboard-row:not([data-layout="full"])  .text-portion {
        background-color: #fff;
    }
    
    .checkerboard [data-layout="full"] .text-portion {
        background-color: transparent;
    }
}

/* Checkerboard: text needs inner padding at tablet/mobile */
/* https://jira.logitech.com/browse/LOGIWEB-1559 */
@media (max-width: 1025px) {
    .checkerboard[data-layout="symmetric"] .text-portion {
        padding: 0 20px;
    }
    
    .checkerboard[data-layout="symmetric"] .copy {
        width: 100%;
        margin-right: 0;

       <script>
        // JavaScript

(function() {
    // LOGIWEB-2140 & 2141
    var waitTime = 25;
    
    var waitForVar = function(key, callback) {
    	if (window[key]) {
    		callback();
    	} else {
    		setTimeout(function() {
    			waitForVar(key, callback);
    		}, waitTime);
    	}
    };
    
    waitForVar('pangea', function() {
        // https://jira.logitech.com/browse/LOGIWEB-2932
        // fix for bundles incorrect label output in selects
        $('.js-bundle .js-select-ctn option').each((i, el) => {
            var label = $(el).attr('data-label');
            $(el).html(label);
        });
        $('.js-bundle .js-other-facets').each((i, el) => {
            $(el).on('facet-selector-update-valid', function(e) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    $(this).find('.js-select-ctn option').each((i, el) => {
                        if ($(el).attr('disabled') !== undefined) {
                            $(el).html($(el).attr('data-label') + ' (' + Granite.I18n.get('not.available.offer') + ')');
                        }
                    });
                }, 50);
        
            });
        });
        
        // https://jira.logitech.com/browse/LOGIWEB-3342
        // fix for broken images in bundles
        $('.js-bundle-item').each((i, elm) => {
        	const $elm = $(elm);
        	const $productShot = $elm.find('.js-bundle-product-shot');
        	const productInfo = JSON.parse($elm.attr('data-productinfo'));
        	const imageSource = productInfo.variants[0].carouselImages[0];
        	const img = imageSource['bundle'];
        	if (!$productShot.find('img').attr('src')) {
        		$productShot.find('img').attr('src', img);
        	}
        });

        
    	// Grab the first banner found on the page.
    	// This safe because this hack works specifically on the homepage, and we know
    	// banner is the top most element.
    	
    	
    	if ($('body').hasClass('homepage')) {
    	    const currentBreakpoint = window.pangea.getCurrentBreakpoint(false);
        	const themeAttribute = 'theme-' + currentBreakpoint;
        	
        	let bannerTheme = $('.js-pangea-banner')
        		.eq(0)
        		.data(themeAttribute);
        
        	// Nav is backwards for some reason....
        	if (bannerTheme === 'theme-dark') {
        		bannerTheme = 'theme-light';
        	} else {
        		bannerTheme = 'theme-dark';
        	}
        	
        	$('.primary-nav-container, .secondary-nav-container')
        		.removeClass('theme-dark-opaque')
        		.removeClass('theme-light-opaque')
        		.removeClass('theme-light')
        		.removeClass('theme-dark')
        		.addClass(bannerTheme);
    	    }
        
    
    });
})();
(function() {
    function init() {
        
    }
 
    // Wait until DOM is ready
    function waitUntilReady(callback) {
        if(document.readyState != 'loading') {
            callback.call(this);
        } else {
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', callback.call(this));
        }
    }
 
    waitUntilReady(init);
})();
       </script>
      </div>

     <script>
      // JavaScript
(function() {
    let $logo;
    let $logoMobile;
    let $logiAni;

    waitUntilReady(init);
    
    // Wait until the libraries we need are ready
    function waitUntilReady(callback) {
        if(document.readyState != 'loading' && window.jQuery) {
            callback.call(this);
        } else {
            setTimeout(() => {
                waitUntilReady(callback);
            }, 50);
        }
    }
    
    function init() {
        if(document.body.classList.contains('wcm-publish') !== true) {
            return;
        }
        
        const locale = window.pangea.getLocale();
        const $mobileLogo = $('.mobile-logo').clone();
        
        if (locale === 'ja-jp' || locale === 'zh-CN') {
            $('.hero-logo-container').before($mobileLogo.addClass('hero-logo-container copy'));
            $('.hero-logo-container:not(.copy)').remove();
            return
        }
        
        $('.author-instructions').remove();
        
        // Replace the logo with the animated version
        $logo = $('#hero-logo-container');
        $logoMobile = $('.mobile-logo');
        $logo.html('<div id="hero-logo-ani" class="hero-logo-ani animating stoppedAnimation"></div>');
        $logoMobile.html('<img class="mobile-dark-logo" src="/content/dam/logitech/common/en/logi-logo-dark.png" alt="logo"><img class="mobile-light-logo" src="/content/dam/logitech/common/en/logi-logo-white.png" alt="logo">');
        $logiAni = $("#hero-logo-ani");
        
        $logo.css('visibility', 'visible');
        
        $logo.hover(
            function() {
                $logiAni
                    .removeClass("stoppedAnimation")
                    .addClass("hoverPlay");
            },
            function() {
                $logiAni
                    .removeClass("hoverPlay")
                    .addClass("stoppedAnimation");
            }
        );
    }
})();
     </script>

         <script>
          // JavaScript
window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(e) {    
	const maxTries = 20;
	let numTries = 0;
	testForJquery();
	function testForJquery() {
		if (typeof jQuery == 'undefined') {
			if (numTries++ < maxTries) {
				setTimeout(testForJquery, 300);
			}
			return;
		} else {
			init();
		}
	};
	function init() {
		let ctnCount = 1;
		$('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e .section-container .content-ctn').each( function() {
			$(this).addClass('content-ctn-' + ctnCount);
			if (ctnCount == 1) {
			 //   console.log('this is', $(this).attr('class'), $(this).closest('.section-container').attr('id'));
			    $(this).closest('.section-container').closest('div:not(.section-container)').addClass('active');
			}
			ctnCount ++;
		});

		$('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e .section-container').each( function() {
			$(this).find('.component-title').closest('div').detach().prependTo($(this));
		});

		$('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e').append('<button class="arrow-button arrow-prev" aria-label="Previous Page"></button><button class="arrow-button arrow-next" aria-label="Next Page"></button>');

		$('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e').find('.arrow-button').click( function() {
			const isNext = $(this).attr('class').search('next');
// 			console.log('isNext', isNext);
			if (isNext > 0) {
				const activeCtn = $('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e .active');
				const nextCtn = $('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e .active').next();
				// console.log("activeCtn", activeCtn.find('.content-ctn').attr('class'));
				// console.log("nextCtn", nextCtn.find('.content-ctn').attr('class'));
				if(nextCtn.length) {
    				const nextOffset = $('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e > .no-container > .aem-padding-options').offset().left - nextCtn.offset().left;
    				// console.log('nextOffset', nextOffset);
    				$('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e > .no-container > .aem-padding-options').css({
    				   transform: 'translateX(' + nextOffset + 'px)' 
    				});
    				nextCtn.addClass('active');
    				activeCtn.removeClass('active');
				}
				$('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e .arrow-prev').fadeIn(250);
				if(!nextCtn.next().length) {
				    $('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e .arrow-next').fadeOut(250);
				}
			} else {
				const activeCtn = $('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e .active');
				const prevCtn = $('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e .active').prev();
				// console.log("activeCtn", activeCtn.find('.content-ctn').attr('class'));
				// console.log("prevCtn", prevCtn.find('.content-ctn').attr('class'));
				if(prevCtn.length) {
    				const prevOffset = $('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e > .no-container > .aem-padding-options').offset().left - prevCtn.offset().left;
    				console.log('prevOffset', prevOffset);
    				$('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e > .no-container > .aem-padding-options').css({
    				   transform: 'translateX(' + prevOffset + 'px)' 
    				});
    				prevCtn.addClass('active');
    				activeCtn.removeClass('active');
				}
				$('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e .arrow-next').fadeIn(250);
				if(!prevCtn.prev().length) {
				    $('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e .arrow-prev').fadeOut(250);
				}
			}
		});
		
		if ($(window).width() > 1024) {
    		$('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e').find('.content-ctn:not(.content-ctn-3) img').each( function() {
    			let alt = $(this).attr('alt');
    			$(this).attr('alt', '');
    			$(this).closest('a').append('<span class="copy-ctn">' + alt + '</span>');
    		});
		}
		$('#ib99f212e3b864081a75bc199fc82469e').addClass('container-xl');
	};
});
         </script>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
    </div>
